    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (isSharpObject ?o)
    (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r)
    (isFridgeReceptacle ?r)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isFridgeReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types agent object receptacle sharpObject - object microwaveReceptacle - receptacle sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle)
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (isSharpObject ?o)
    (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r)
    (isFridgeReceptacle ?r)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isFridgeReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o) (isSharpObject ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types agent object receptacle sharpObject - object microwaveReceptacle - receptacle sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle)
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (isSharpObject ?o)
    (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r)
    (isFridgeReceptacle ?r)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isFridgeReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o) (isSharpObject ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

 )

 )

 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))

 )

    (isFridgeReceptacle ?r)
 )

 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (isMicrowaveReceptacle ?r))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)

    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject

    object

    receptacle - object

    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)

    (sliced ?o - object)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)

    object

    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle

 )

    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)

    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)

    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)

    (sliced ?o - object)
 )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))

            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject

    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))

 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)

    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)

    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)

    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent - object
    receptacle - object
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    object
    agent
    receptacle
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (atAgentReceptacle ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions (total-cost) - number)
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?from)) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (pickupable ?o) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (holds ?a ?o) (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r)) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (inReceptacle ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (when (on ?o) (not (on ?o))) (when (not (on ?o)) (on ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cleaned ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (atAgentReceptacle ?a ?r) (inReceptacle ?co ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
)
